## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics (classical mechanics)
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, where dv_dt depends on position x, velocity v, and possibly time t. The relationship encodes restoring forces, damping, and potential driving terms characteristic of well-known nonlinear oscillator models.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (Duffing + damping)
- Quintic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinearity)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x**2 * v (nonlinear damping)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (velocity-dependent nonlinear damping)
- Driven Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (forced nonlinear oscillator)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = (c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x (time-modulated stiffness)
- Generalized nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * x**2 * v + c4 * x * v**2 (mixed nonlinear terms)
- Softening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2) (position-dependent stiffness)
- Nonlinear damped driven: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * (1 + c3 * x**2) * v + c4 * sin(c5 * t) (full nonlinear model)
- Cubic damping with restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v * x**2 + c3 * v**3 (combined nonlinearities)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x┬│, xŌüĄ) preserve symmetry of oscillation about equilibrium ŌĆö use odd polynomial in x
- Amplitude-dependent frequency shift suggests cubic or higher odd-power terms in x (Duffing-type nonlinearity)
- Self-sustained oscillations (limit cycles) imply velocity terms with sign changes, e.g., (1 - x┬▓)*v structure (Van der Pol)
- Energy-dependent damping manifests as products of position powers and velocity: x┬▓*v or v┬│ terms
- Periodic driving forces appear as sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) additive terms independent of x and v
- Parametric excitation couples time-dependence multiplicatively with position: cos(c*t)*x
- If the system is autonomous (no explicit t dependence), dv_dt should only involve x and v
- Hamiltonian (conservative) systems have dv_dt depending only on x (no v terms), derivable from a potential V(x)
